## <a name="windows-server-2012"></a><span data-ttu-id="251e8-1799">Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="251e8-1799">Windows Server 2012</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="251e8-1800">Атрибуты</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="251e8-1800">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2012-attributes)
